Codelco has 8 sites.\n\n\n\nRate the level of impact to acQuire business\n\n\n\n(if applicable)\n\n\n\n1: Minimal, customer will continue to buy\n\n\n\nCan you quantify the impact:\n\n\n\nAnnual Maintenance value: N/A\n\n\n\nBD opportunity value: N/A\n\n\n\nCS opportunity value: More Monitoring licenses OPP are in progress.\n\n\n\nUSD  7,328 in Maintenance\n\n\n\nWorkaround(s)\n\n\n\n \n\n\n\n[Implication]\n\n\n\nCurrently, in DrillholeTemporalMonitoring we associate the EVENT with reading, through a virtual field (Example: MN_EVENTNAME) but we would like the association to be natural.\n\n\n\nIt is not a FOREING KEY constraint, is not natural for a relational database\n\n\n\nDrillholeTemporalMonitoring\n\n\n\n\t\n\nMONITORINGNAME\n\n\n\nREADTIME\n\n\n\nMN_Level\n\n\n\nMN_Ph\n\n\n\nMN_EVENTNAME\n\n\n\nPZO-01\n\n\n\n9/1/17 8:00\n\n\n\n                    3,450.00 \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nBOMBEO_2017\n\n\n\nPZO-01\n\n\n\n9/2/17 8:10\n\n\n\n                    3,448.00 \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nPZO-01\n\n\n\n9/6/17 8:20\n\n\n\n \n\n\n\n                                 5.60 \n\n\n\nBOMBEO_2017\n\n\n\nPZO-01\n\n\n\n9/3/17 8:20\n\n\n\n                    3,446.00 \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nPZO-01\n\n\n\n9/4/17 8:30\n\n\n\n                    3,444.00 \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nBOMBEO_2017\n\n\n\nPZO-01\n\n\n\n9/5/17 8:40\n\n\n\n                    3,442.00 \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nPZO-02\n\n\n\n9/1/17 8:00\n\n\n\n                    3,450.00 \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nBOMBEO_2017\n\n\n\nPZO-02\n\n\n\n9/2/17 8:10\n\n\n\n                    3,448.00 \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nBOMBEO_2017\n\n\n\nPZO-02\n\n\n\n9/3/17 8:20\n\n\n\n                    3,446.00 \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nBOMBEO_2017\n\n\n\nPZO-02\n\n\n\n9/4/17 8:30\n\n\n\n                    3,444.00 \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nBOMBEO_2017\n\n\n\nPZO-02\n\n\n\n9/5/17 8:40\n\n\n\n                    3,442.00 \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nBOMBEO_2017\n\n\n\nAdditional Comments\n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nv4.1\n\n\n\n \n\n\n\n\n\nUser Story Creation Guide - Please Read\n\n\n\n\n\nGoals\n\n\n\n\n\n1.       Implementation and Technology Agnostic (within practicality)\n\n\n\n2.       Provides Context, a reason and cause for the user engaging in the activity\n\n\n\n3.       Details a sufficient amount of information as to allow a developer to code against it and a tester to test against it.\n\n\n\n\n\nRules of Thumb\n\n\n\n\n\n·         Balanced: Avoid doing exactly what the user asks for and avoid deciding you know better than the user.\n\n\n\n·         Complete Story: \n\n\n\no   Who: is always only one person\n\n\n\no   What: is always only one thing they want to achieve \n\n\n\no   Why: why this outcome matters to the user.\n\n\n\n·         Acceptance Criteria: a clearly expressing a user\x19 s expected experience from and action\n\n\n\n·         Visualized: When in doubt write out like a movie of comic book strip. If you cannot draw it based on your description, a developer cannot develop it based on that description.\n\n\n\n·         Apportioned: When in doubt make it an Epic. (Each feature should have an epic).\n\n\n\n\n\nI.N.V.E.S.T\n\n\n\n\n\n·         Independent: means it describes the whole process from cause of desire to outcome\n\n\n\n·         Negotiable: Keep the details of the ticket something discussable with a developer, do not specify what actions a developer must take, only what they must achieve.\n\n\n\n·         Valuable: There should be a defined relatable value to the user / purchaser. A clear reason for engaging in the activity, understandable by almost anyone.\n\n\n\n·         Estimable: The story should be enough that a developer could understand all the things that must be done in order to realise the outcome for the user and list them.\n\n\n\n·         Small: each story should detail only one interaction with the product.\n\n\n\n·         Testable: ensure enough detail on how the \x1c who\x1d  would know if it worked.\n\n\n\n\n\nTemplate\n\n\n\n\n\nUser Story\n\n\n\n\n\nAs a [Type of User] \n\n\n\nI want to [Action taken]\n\n\n\nSo that [Cause of the action to be taken]\n\n\n\n\n\nAcceptance Criteria\n\n\n\n\n\nGiven [The state of the product]\n\n\n\nWhen [The action taken by the user]\n\n\n\nThen [The expected behaviour of the product]\n\n\n\n\n\nWords to Avoid\n\n\n\n\n\nFast, Seamless, Natural, Obvious, Correct, Appropriate, Logical, Normal, Common Sense, Intuitive, etc.\n\n\n\nIf you cannot draw it based on that word, a developer cannot develop it based on that word.\n\n\n\n \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\n \n\n\n\nAna Sampaio ACP GDA\n\n\n\nGeoscientific Data Analyst\n\n\n\nacQuire Technology Solutions Pty Ltd\n\n\n\nT: \n\n\n\n+56 2 2203 4072 <tel:+56%202%202203%204072> \n\n\n\nE: \n\n\n\na.sampaio@acquire.com.au <mailto:a.sampaio@acquire.com.au> \n\n\n\nW: \n\n\n\nwww.acquire.com.au <http://www.acquire.com.au> \n\n\n\nAmapolas 1290, oficina 101, 7510308 Providencia, Región Metropolitana, Chile <http://www.acquire.com.au> \n\n\n\nAUSTRALIA | CANADA | CHILE | SOUTH AFRICA\n\n\n\nGIM Suite Starter (1000) \x13  Santiago \x13  Oct 2nd to 5th 2017 \n\nGIM Suite Practitioner (2000) -
